</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тля</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pétlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: small loop, small noose</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>петля́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petljá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: small loop, small noose</li>
<li>eyelet, eye, pull strap, tab</li></ol>

***петля.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>петля</a> (3945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*petьľa</i>, from an Old Germanic i-umlauted form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fatilaz</i>: compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">fetill</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">fezzil</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fessel</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">fetel</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fettle</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тля</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>петля́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pétlja</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">petljá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тли</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>петли́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тель</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>loop <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">length of thread, line or rope, a shape produced by a curve</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>noose</li>
<li>buttonhole, eye</li>
<li>stitch</li>
<li>hinge</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:петроградский.html>петрогра́дский</a></b>

***петрушка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:петрушка.html>петру́шка</a> (16175)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">pietruszka</i>, adapted from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">petržel</i> (see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́шка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-úška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">petersîlje</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">petroselīnum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πετροσέλῑνον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petrosélīnon</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rock celery</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">parsley</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петрушка.html>петру́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">petrúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петрушка.html>петру́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петрушка.html>петру́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петрушка.html>петру́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> parsley (herb)</li>
<li>foolishness, absurdity</li></ol>

***петух.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>пету́х</a> (3765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>петь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ух</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ux</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, said to have been influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>пе́тя</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Pétja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">Пётр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Pjotr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>петь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пе́вень</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pévenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">пі́вень</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pívenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">пе́вень</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pjévjenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">пете́л</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petél</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macedonian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Macedonian language">Macedonian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mk">петел</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petel</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">pijétao</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">pijévac</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">petêlin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">pẹ́təł</i>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">piać</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to crow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>петь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Likewise <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">canere</i> means both “to sing” and “to crow”.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>пету́х</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">petúx</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>петуха́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>петухи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>петухо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rooster, cock
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>пету́х</a></b> укаре́кает: кукареку́!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Petúx</b> ukarékajet: kukarekú!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The <b>rooster</b> is crowing: cock-a-doodle-doo!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>пету́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>то́пчет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курица.html>ку́рицу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Petúx</b> tópčet kúricu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The <b>rooster</b> is mounting a hen.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">very  rare<span class="ib-comma">,</span> easily confused with slang meaning</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> impulsive, aggressive person or group
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b>,  Владислав Бахревский (Vladislav Bakhrevsky),  <cite>Люба <a href = vnd.unilang:украина.html>Укра́ина</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>До́лгий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a></cite>, LitRes, <small>→ISBN</small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казаки́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задохнуться.html>задохну́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́ха</a>: — <a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>пету́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>пету́х</a></b>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́ши</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лости</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:вскричать.html>вскрича́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаянье.html>отча́янье</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гонец.html>гоне́ц</a>. — <a href = vnd.unilang:казак.html>казаки́</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:присланный.html>при́слан</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сообщить.html>сообщи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вам</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:величество.html>вели́чество</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:король.html>коро́ль</a> владисла́в IV <a href = vnd.unilang:умереть.html>у́мер</a>. хмельни́цкий а́же <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прикрыть.html>прикры́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>ве́ками</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:сколь.html>сколь</a> ...</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kazakí zadoxnúlisʹ ot sméxa: — Nu, <b>petúx</b> i <b>petúx</b>! — Váši mílosti! — vskričál v otčájanʹje gonéc. — Kazakí! Ja príslan soobščítʹ vam, što jevó velíčestvo korólʹ Vladisláv IV úmer. Xmelʹníckij áže glazá prikrýl vékami: skolʹ ...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The Cossacks laughed until they were gasping for air: "Well, a <b>rooster</b> and a <b>rooster</b>!" "Your Graces!", cried the messenger in despair. "Cossacks! I am sent to inform you that His Majesty King Vladislav IV has died. Khmelnitsky even closed his eyes: how...</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang, believed to be  criminal slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> passive homosexual male</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">ellipsis of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">га́лльский <a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>пету́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Gállʹskij petúx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:петушок.html>петушок</a> (8415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петушок.html>петушо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">petušók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петушок.html>петушка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петушок.html>петушки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петушок.html>петушко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>пету́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">petúx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (young) rooster</li>
<li>fighting fish, betta</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> passive gay</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>петь</a> (776)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pěti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*PoiH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>петь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">petʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропеть.html>пропе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sing</li>
<li>to crow</li></ol>

***пехота.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пехота.html>пехо́та</a> (4273)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pěxъ</i>, which is derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pēd-</i>, a variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ped-</i>.
Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">floor, ground</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пехота.html>пехо́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pexóta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пехота.html>пехо́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пехота.html>пехо́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пехота.html>пехо́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>infantry</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">печа́лить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečálitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печалиться.html>печа́литься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pečálitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опеча́литься</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be sad, to grieve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:печалиться.html>печа́литься</a></b> ра́ньше <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pečálitʹsja</b> ránʹše vrémeni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to meet trouble halfway</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">печа́лить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečálitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***печаль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ль</a> (4346)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečalĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">grief, censern, loathing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pečalь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pekti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pečálʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sadness, grief, sorrow
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1829</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Pushkin" class="extiw" title="w:Alexander Pushkin">Alexander Pushkin</a>,  “На <a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>холмах</a> Грузии...  | On the hills of Georgia ... | ”, in <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://max.mmlc.northwestern.edu/~mdenner/Demo/texts/on_hills_georgia.htm">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>хо́лмах</a> гру́зии <a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежи́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночной.html>ночна́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мгла.html>мгла́</a>;<br /> <a href = vnd.unilang:шуметь.html>шуми́т</a> ара́гва <a href = vnd.unilang:предо.html>пре́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мно́ю</a>.<br /> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грустно.html>гру́стно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:легко.html>легко́</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ль</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:светлый.html>светла́</a>;<br /> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ль</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>полна́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тобо́ю</a>,<br /> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тобо́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тобо́й</a>... уны́нья <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моего́</a><br /> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чит</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тревожить.html>трево́жит</a>,<br /> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вновь.html>вно́вь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>гори́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>лю́бит</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:оттого.html>оттого́</a>,<br /> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>оно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na xólmax Grúzii ležít nočnája mglá;<br /> Šumít Arágva prédo mnóju.<br /> Mne grústno i lexkó; <b>pečálʹ</b> mojá svetlá;<br /> <b>Pečálʹ</b> mojá polná tobóju,<br /> Tobój, odnój tobój... Unýnʹja mojevó<br /> Ništó ne múčit, ne trevóžit,<br /> I sérdce vnóvʹ gorít i ljúbit — ottovó,<br /> Što ne ljubítʹ onó ne móžet.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Dark falls upon the hills of Georgia,<br /> I hear Aragva's roar.<br /> I'm sad and light, my grief—transparent,<br /> My sorrow is suffused with you,<br /> With you, with you alone...My melancholy<br /> Remains untouched and undisturbed,<br /> And once again my heart ignites and loves<br /> Because it can't do otherwise.</span></dd><dl><dd><span class="e-footer">(The accent of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холм.html>хо́лмах</a></span> is Church Slavonic.)</span></dd></dl></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ча́ль</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:печальный.html>печа́льный</a> (1904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печаль.html>печа́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečálʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печальный.html>печа́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pečálʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sad, grieved, sorrowful, wistful, doleful, mournful</li>
<li>grievous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печальный.html>печа́льный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конец.html>коне́ц</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pečálʹnyj konéc</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dismal end, bad end</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тать</a> (4391)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pečátatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напечатать.html>напеча́тать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распечатать.html>распеча́тать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to print <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to copy something on a surface, especially by machine</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:распечатать.html>распеча́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">raspečátatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also, especially on a printer</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to type <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to use a typewriter or to enter text or commands into a computer using a keyboard</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***печать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́ть</a> (1940)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pečátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́тей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>seal, stamp</li>
<li>press</li>
<li>print, type</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 3; -moz-column-count: 3; -ms-column-count: 3; -o-column-count: 3; -webkit-column-count: 3;">

***печень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́чень</a> (4417)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́чень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečenĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печеный.html>печёный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">печі́нка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečínka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">pieczeń</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">pečenka</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">roast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">kẽpenys</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">liver</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">kèpti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́чень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péčenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́чени</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́чени</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́ченей</a></b>)

***печенье.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:печенье.html>пече́нье</a> (9961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>пе́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">péčʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Proto-Indo-European <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pekʷ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cook</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">biscuit</i> (in part).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печенье.html>пече́нье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pečénʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печенье.html>пече́нья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печенье.html>пече́нья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печенье.html>пече́ний</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пече́нька</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pastry, cruller</li>
<li>cookie (U.S.), biscuit (U.K.)</li>
<li>cracker</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***печь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a> (14838)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*peťi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pekʷ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cook</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">culinary</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cuisine</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">concoct</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">peptic</i>.
Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пот.html>пот</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pot</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sweat, perspiration</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">पचति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pácati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq">pjek</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tocharian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Tocharian languages">Tocharian B</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="txb">päk-</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πέσσω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">péssō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">coquō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испечь.html>испе́чь</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">спечь</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bake</li>
<li>to scorch <i>(said of the sun)</i></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*peťь</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пещь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peščʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span>.
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>пе́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>пе́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>пече́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stove</li>
<li>oven</li>
<li>furnace
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">кали́льная <b><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kalílʹnaja <b>pečʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">heating/calcining <b>furnace</b>; calciner</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>kiln</li></ol>
